Okay, so we're going to start with pattern breaking. And this part is separated into two parts, 4 in five. Pattern breaking, the first one here, we can start by making a totally counterintuitive phrase, and I 'll show you an example here now. But I want you to understand that when you start a VSL, a sales video, not just a sales video itself, any type of copy, we will always first seek to grab the person's attention. That's the initial objective because if... If we don't get our lead's attention, they won't consume the rest of our copy, our sales letter, our VSL. Consequently, our VSL, however incredible it may be, will be useless if the person doesn't watch it. So, here's the pattern break. What is a pattern break? It's precisely showing something counterintuitive, something that grabs the person's attention. The person is like, "Wait, what's happening here?" Today, in this social media age, there's a huge competition for attention, which is one of the biggest assets, if not the biggest asset, in our current reality.
